# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [CADENZA in Action: Breaking the Monolith with Intent-Dependent Plan Spaces for Semantic Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01468)
*Jaehyun Ha,Yongjoo Park,Wook-Shin Han*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: CADENZA是一个语义查询优化器，通过将自然语言意图分解为步骤、选择具体物理实现并调参，在用户指定的质量-延迟-成本偏好下优化语义算子执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化器以整体粒度优化语义算子（如LLM、嵌入模型），导致代价高昂的模型调用与无法捕捉意图语义的廉价替代方案之间难以权衡。

Method: 将意图分解为多个步骤，为每一步选择具体物理实现，并在用户指定的质量-延迟-成本偏好下调优参数。

Result: 通过Web界面展示意图如何分解为候选计划、每个计划如何优化，以及不同偏好如何产生不同的最优计划。

Conclusion: CADENZA通过细粒度分解与优化，突破了传统整体式优化器的局限，实现了更灵活的语义查询优化。

Abstract: Semantic query processing engines execute semantic operators, whose behavior is specified by natural-language intents, via model inference over multimodal data. Most existing optimizers optimize the operators at the granularity of monolithic implementations -- such as LLMs and embedding models -- forcing a trade-off between expensive model calls and cheaper alternatives that fail to capture intent-dependent semantics. We present CADENZA, a semantic operator optimizer that compiles an intent into decomposed steps, selects concrete physical implementations for each step, and tunes their parameters under user-specified quality-latency-cost preferences. In this demonstration, users interact with CADENZA through a web interface over multimodal databases, exploring how an intent is decomposed into alternative plans, how each plan is optimized, and how different preferences yield different winning plans.

</details>


### [2] [The General Stability of Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01546)
*Houming Chen,H. V. Jagadish*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文提出通用稳定性（General Stability），将传统严格匹配的排名稳定性推广为基于距离的度量，允许用户定义排名变化的重要性，并开发了相应的计算算法（二维扫描、无偏多维采样、Conv-SC），在八个真实数据集上验证了方法的有效性和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统排名稳定性要求权重扰动后排名完全不变，这种严格匹配过于粗糙——轻微扰动导致底部项交换即判为不稳定，无法区分"重大变化"与"微小变化"。需要一种允许用户自定义排名变化重要性的更灵活的稳定性度量。

Method: 1) 形式化定义通用稳定性（General Stability），聚合排名区域并按用户定义的距离函数加权；2) 提出二维扫描算法和无偏多维采样算法；3) 针对高维可扩展性问题，识别拟凸距离函数子类，提出Conv-SC算法将稳定性计算转化为凸体积近似问题（多项式时间可解）。

Result: 在八个真实数据集和生成数据上的实验表明：距离敏感的稳定性能提供更丰富的信息；所提出的估计器准确且实用；Conv-SC在拟凸距离函数下显著改善了随维度增长的扩展性。

Conclusion: 通用稳定性是对传统精确稳定性的有意义推广，提供了灵活的框架；拟凸距离函数子类具有良好计算性质，可通过凸体积近似高效求解；为排名稳定性分析开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Rankings derived from weighted scoring functions are widely used in settings such as university rankings and employment candidate evaluations. Since ranking weights are often chosen by organizations or analysts, ranking stability asks whether a reported ranking persists under reasonable weight changes. Prior work on stable rankings formalizes this idea through volume-based stability, which measures the fraction of the weight space that induces the target ranking exactly.
  This exact-match requirement can be too blunt: once a perturbed weight vector produces a different ranking, exact stability gives it no credit, whether the change replaces the top-ranked item or only swaps two nearly tied lower-ranked items. We propose general stability, a distance-based generalization that aggregates ranking regions according to a user-defined distance from the target ranking. This lets users specify which ranking changes matter in the application, while recovering exact stability as a special case.
  Our algorithmic focus is stability computation: given a reported or user-specified ranking and a distance function, estimate its general-stability score. We give a two-dimensional sweep algorithm and an unbiased multidimensional sampler that extend exact-stability methods, and analyze why sampling can scale poorly as the dimension grows. Motivated by this scaling challenge, we identify quasiconvex distance functions as a tractable subclass and introduce Conv-SC, which reduces stability computation for this subclass to convex-volume approximation, where randomized polynomial-time methods are available. Experiments on eight real datasets and generated instances show that distance-sensitive stability gives informative real-data results, that our estimators are accurate and practical, and that Conv-SC improves scaling with dimension for quasiconvex distance functions.

</details>


### [3] [pykci: A Compact Urban Knowledge Graph for Semantic and Spatial Queries using LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01605)
*Huynh Duc An Son Nguyen,Lukas Arzoumanidis,Youness Dehbi*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: pykci是一个将CityGML 2.0城市3D模型转换为Neo4j知识图谱的开源系统，支持自然语言查询，无需用户掌握查询语言或数据库专业知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CityGML标准虽能建模丰富的语义3D城市模型，但其XML编码和关系数据库映射导致数据难以直接查询，需要专家知识，限制了城市规划师、GIS从业者和市民的访问。

Method: 开发pykci系统：①将CityGML 2.0数据集转换为Neo4j知识图谱（覆盖所有主题特征模块和细节层级，R-tree空间索引）；②构建端到端Python管道（数据入库→导出为3D Tiles可视化→无损回导出CityGML）；③通过模型无关的text-to-Cypher机制，将图模式作为上下文，由大语言模型将自然语言问题翻译为Cypher查询。

Result: 在德国汉堡的CityGML LoD2开放数据集上验证，成功处理复杂语义和空间查询（如识别适合绿化的屋顶表面）。支持本地开源模型（保护敏感数据）和商用模型两种方案，答案基于真实城市数据而非模型记忆，减少幻觉并提供可审计溯源。

Conclusion: pykci降低了语义3D城市模型的使用门槛，使非专家用户也能通过自然语言交互进行查询，同时保持数据准确性和可追溯性。

Abstract: CityGML, the OGC standard for modeling, storage, and exchange of semantic 3D city models, describes urban objects with detailed semantics, geometry, and topology. Yet this richness is difficult to query directly: CityGML's XML encoding is designed for exchange rather than analysis, and relational mappings expose it through schemas requiring expert knowledge. We present pykci (Python Knowledge Graph for Cities), an open-source system that transforms CityGML 2.0 datasets into a compact urban knowledge graph in Neo4j and makes it queryable in natural language. The graph schema covers all thematic feature modules of CityGML 2.0 across all levels of detail and is spatially indexed with an R-tree for efficient geometric retrieval. A complete end-to-end Python pipeline ingests CityGML datasets into the knowledge graph, exports them to OGC 3D Tiles for interactive visualization, and supports lossless round-trip export of all content back to CityGML. For querying, the graph is paired with a large language model through a model-agnostic text-to-Cypher mechanism: the graph schema is supplied as context, and the model translates natural-language questions into Cypher queries executed against the graph. We evaluate both a locally running open-weight model, which keeps sensitive city data on-premise, and a state-of-the-art commercial model for the most demanding spatial and semantic queries. Answers are grounded in exact city data rather than the model's parametric memory, reducing hallucination and providing auditable provenance for every response. We demonstrate the system on open-government CityGML LoD2 datasets from Hamburg, Germany, including complex semantic and spatial queries such as identifying roof surfaces suitable for greening. pykci enables urban planners, GIS practitioners, and citizens to interact with semantic 3D city models without expertise in query languages and database schemas.

</details>


### [4] [AgenticDataBench: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Data Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01647)
*Zhaoyan Sun,Shan Zhong,Daizhou Wen,Jiaxing Han,Guoliang Li,Ying Yan,Peng Zhang,Yu Su,Xiang Qi,Baolin Sun,Chengyuan Yang,Tao Fang,Huaiyu Ruan*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出了AgenticDataBench，一个用于评估LLM驱动的数据科学智能体的综合基准，涵盖15个垂直领域和5个真实B2B场景，通过数据科学技能量化覆盖范围，并提供了细粒度的评估框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据科学自动化对减少人工成本至关重要，但现有基于LLM的数据智能体缺乏全面的、细粒度的高质量基准来评估其在不同场景下的性能。

Method: 1) 收集15个垂直领域的真实数据集和任务（含5个B2B案例）；2) 引入数据科学技能概念，利用Stack Overflow任务解决方案进行技能对齐层次聚类；3) 最大化真实任务中技能组成的多样性；4) 基于技能的LLM任务生成方法为缺乏真实数据的领域创建任务。

Result: 构建了AgenticDataBench基准，并评估了当前最先进的数据智能体，提供了细粒度的技能级洞察。

Conclusion: AgenticDataBench填补了数据科学智能体评估领域的空白，通过技能量化和多样化场景覆盖，为未来研究提供了标准化评估平台。

Abstract: Data science aims to derive actionable insights from heterogeneous raw data, unlocking the value of the massive amounts of data generated in modern society. Automating this process is essential to reducing labor-intensive efforts for data scientists and enabling scalable data-driven applications. Recently, large language model (LLM)-based data agents have emerged as a promising solution to automate data science workflows. However, the field lacks comprehensive benchmarks to rigorously evaluate these agents across diverse scenarios with fine-grained granularity. To address this gap, we propose AgenticDataBench, a comprehensive benchmark featuring realistic tasks spanning diverse domains with fine-grained ground-truth labels. This enables evaluations to capture the diversity and complexity of data science workflows and the detailed performance of agents. First, to cover diverse domains, we collect real datasets and tasks from 15 vertical domains, including 5 real-world B2B use cases from a leading fintech company. Second, to remove redundancy in real-world tasks and generate high-quality tasks for domains lacking real data, we introduce data science skills, recurring data-centric operational patterns, and quantify benchmark coverage by the number of skills included. Representative skills are extracted from large-scale task solutions on Stack Overflow using skill-aligned hierarchical clustering. Third, for real-world business tasks, we select task-solution pairs that maximize diversity in skill composition, ensuring broad coverage of practical scenarios. Fourth, to generate realistic tasks for devise domains without real tasks, we propose a systematic LLM-based task generation approach to create workflows and tasks based on these skills. Finally, we evaluate state-of-the-art data agents using our annotated benchmark and open-sourced testbed, providing detailed skill-level insights.

</details>


### [5] [HNSW with Accuracy Guarantees Using Graph Spanners -- A Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02338)
*Minghao Li,Raghav Mittal,Sanjivni Rana,Suraj Shetiya,Gautam Das,Nick Koudas*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出"Certify-then-Rectify"框架，通过统计认证动态评估HNSW搜索质量，仅在必要时切换至精确恢复算法，兼顾HNSW的平均速度与精确搜索的最坏情况正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HNSW虽性能优异但基于贪心遍历缺乏理论正确性保证，现有方法无法兼顾启发式搜索的速度与精确检索的严谨性。

Method: 1) 无分布统计认证器动态评估HNSW搜索质量；2) 低质量时安全升级至精确恢复算法；3) 将HNSW图重解释为几何spanner，利用极值理论随机估计最大经验伸展因子，从而数学上界约束真实最近邻的最大距离。

Result: 在基准数据集上，所提分层框架在平均情况下达到HNSW的速度，同时保证了最坏情况下的精确搜索正确性，优于其他可用方法。

Conclusion: 成功弥合了启发式搜索速度与精确检索严谨性之间的差距，为HNSW提供了理论上的正确性保障。

Abstract: Hierarchical Navigable Small World (HNSW) graphs serve as the industry standard due to their logarithmic complexity and strong empirical performance. However, HNSW relies on greedy graph traversal, a heuristic that provides no theoretical guarantees of correctness. In this paper, we propose a novel "Certify-then-Rectify" framework that bridges the gap between the speed of heuristic search and the rigor of exact retrieval. Rather than discarding HNSW, our approach first employs a distribution-free statistical certifier to dynamically evaluate the quality of a standard HNSW search with minimal overhead. If certification indicates that the retrieved neighbors are of low quality, the framework safely escalates to a rigorous exact recovery algorithm. To make this exact recovery computationally feasible, we reinterpret the HNSW graph as a geometric spanner and utilize Extreme Value Theory to stochastically estimate its maximum empirical stretch factor. This allows us to mathematically bound the maximum distance of true nearest neighbors. Extensive evaluations on benchmark datasets demonstrate that our tiered framework delivers the average-case speed of HNSW while ensuring the worst-case correctness of exact search and outperforming other applicable approaches.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [HYPIC: Accelerating Hybrid-Attention LLM Serving with Position-Independent Caching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01299)
*Yifei Liu,Juntong Wu,Yang Liu,Junhao Hu,Minghao Li,Xiaoxu Chen,Weihang Chen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Hypic是一个针对混合注意力LLM的推理系统，通过引入段累积转移算子和边界窗口重计算机制，实现了位置无关缓存，在保持高准确率的同时将TTFT降低2.45倍、峰值吞吐提升2.0倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG和智能体LLM服务中，提示由独立段组装成长上下文，导致预填充阶段成为计算瓶颈。现有位置无关缓存（PIC）和混合注意力模型两种优化方向无法共存：PIC依赖逐token的KV缓存复用，而混合注意力中的线性注意力层使用逐请求的循环状态，导致PIC的原始操作无法直接迁移。

Method: 1) 在线性注意力层，识别"段累积转移算子"作为缺失的代数原语，缓存该算子及每个段的零起始端状态，实现独立缓存段的近精确常数时间状态组合。2) 在全注意力层，发现注意力偏差集中在段边界，仅重计算边界小窗口即可恢复跨段回溯能力。3) 利用段级自包含性并行化缓存缺失的预填充，将长冷请求转化为可加速的工作负载。

Result: 在四种混合注意力模型和五种工作负载上，Hypic将TTFT平均降低2.45倍，峰值吞吐最高提升2.0倍，准确率与完全重计算相比偏差在3.3个点以内。

Conclusion: Hypic首次实现了混合注意力LLM的位置无关缓存系统，通过为线性注意力层设计新的缓存原语、为全注意力层设计边界重计算机制，以及并行化缓存缺失预填充，成功融合了PIC和混合注意力两种技术路线的优势。

Abstract: In retrieval augmented generation (RAG) and agentic LLM serving, prompts are assembled from independent segments into long contexts, making the prefill stage dominate the per-request computation cost. To this cost, two directions have emerged in parallel: position-independent caching (PIC) admits KV reuse for non-contiguous segments shared across different requests, while hybrid-attention models reduce computation complexity by replacing most full-attention layers with linear attention. However, they cannot coexist: applying PIC to hybrid-attention models breaks down because per-token KV-cache reuse primitives do not transfer to the per-request recurrent state.
  In this work, we present Hypic, the first serving system for hybrid-attention LLMs with position-independent caching. For linear-attention layers, we identify the segment-cumulative transition operator as the missing algebraic primitive, and cache it alongside each segment's zero-start end-state, enabling near-exact and constant-time state composition of independently cached segments. For the remaining full-attention layers, existing PIC methods also fail as linear layers do not expose the per-token hidden states for selective recomputation. We show that the most significant attention deviation concentrates at segment boundaries, so recomputing only a small seam window at each boundary suffices to restore cross-segment lookback. Finally, Hypic exploits segment-level self-containment to parallelize cache-miss prefill across instances, turning long cold requests -- a major tail-latency contributor under both prefix caching and prior PIC -- into an accelerable workload. Evaluated across four hybrid-attention models and five workloads, Hypic reduces time-to-first-token (TTFT) by 2.45x on average and improves peak throughput by up to 2.0x over existing systems, while staying within 3.3 points of full-recompute accuracy.

</details>


### [7] [SLFS: a Flexible, Low-Cost Distributed File System Using Serverless Designs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01486)
*Cheng Hao,Yang,Paola Alsharabaty,Soufiane Jounaid,Cristina Nita-Rotaru,Ji-Yong Shin*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: SLFS是利用无服务器函数构建的分布式文件系统，支持毫秒级弹性扩缩容，通过多线程短生命周期服务器设计解决冷启动问题，相比λFS、EFS和Ceph分别降低最高63%、68%和63%的成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统分布式文件系统为应对峰值负载过度预配资源，而现有扩缩容机制粒度过粗（以整台服务器为单位）、速度过慢（分钟到小时级），无法跟踪文件系统常见的快速、细粒度负载变化。

Method: 基于无服务器函数（serverless functions）构建分布式文件系统的数据与元数据操作；利用键值存储实现简单短小的函数操作；提出多线程短生命周期服务器设计克服冷启动问题；通过策略协调器将文件映射到函数实例、弹性扩缩容并控制函数生命周期以平衡性能与成本；支持多种存储后端（S3等云原生服务或用户管理的键值存储）。

Result: 相比基础无服务器设计，冷启动问题减轻580倍；相比λFS、EFS和Ceph，分别以最高63%、68%和63%的更优成本实现更优或相当性能。

Conclusion: SLFS证明了无服务器计算可以高效构建分布式文件系统，实现细粒度弹性与低成本，但依赖键值存储等后端服务，且多线程短生命周期设计虽缓解但未完全消除冷启动开销。

Abstract: Large-scale distributed file systems must provision resources for peak demand, yet file access patterns fluctuate significantly, leaving substantial capacity idle during off-peak periods. Existing scaling mechanisms operate at the granularity of entire servers and take minutes to hours, making them unable to track the rapid, fine-grained load variations that file systems commonly experience. Serverless computing, with its millisecond-granularity elasticity and pay-per-use pricing, offers a compelling alternative. We present SLFS, the first distributed file system built with serverless functions for both data and metadata operations. SLFS implements file services on top of key-value stores, keeping function operations simple and short, and introduces a novel multi-threaded, short-lived server design that overcomes the cold-start problem while maintaining low cost. A policy-enforcing coordinator efficiently maps files to function instances, scales the system elastically, and controls function lifetimes to balance performance and cost. SLFS can flexibly run on diverse storage backends -- from cloud-native services like S3 to user-managed key-value stores -- enabling configurable cost-performance trade-offs. Our evaluation shows that SLFS mitigates cold starts by 580$\times$ compared to the base serverless design and outperforms $λ$FS, EFS, and Ceph at up to 63%, 68%, and 63% lower cost, respectively.

</details>


### [8] [OmniPilot: An Uncertainty-Aware LLM Inference Advisor for Heterogeneous GPU Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01579)
*D. Balamurugan,Thomas W. Bush*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出OmniPilot，一个面向异构GPU集群的LLM服务配置推荐系统，通过校准的量化成本模型与分布外弃权层，在A100/H100/H200等硬件上实现6.2%的吞吐量预测误差与95%的Top-1配置准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在共享异构GPU集群上部署LLM时，用户需要选择GPU类型、张量并行度与精度等配置，但有效吞吐量、启动成功率及集群需求持续波动，静态配置方案无法捕捉量化与模型家族的交互、KV缓存与精度的权衡等关键因素，且硬件故障频发，亟需动态配置推荐方案。

Method: OmniPilot包含两个核心组件：1) 经过保形校准的分位数成本模型，覆盖8个服务目标；2) 分布外(OOD)弃权层。系统通过经济效用指标（校准至操作者的显示偏好）对配置进行排序，当请求超出模型支持的测量范围时主动弃权。

Result: 在460次基准测试中（涵盖A100/H100/H200及四种精度），OmniPilot的聚合吞吐量预测MAPE为6.2%，log空间R²=0.92；Top-1准确率达95%，平均效用遗憾仅0.003。在OOD测试集上预测误差升至24-46%，但弃权层成功识别全部5个低置信度样本。

Conclusion: OmniPilot通过保形校准与OOD弃权机制实现了高精度的配置推荐，并能通过持续吸收OOD场景扩展支持范围，为异构GPU集群上的LLM服务部署提供了实用的决策支持工具。

Abstract: Serving large language models (LLMs) on a shared, heterogeneous GPU cluster requires users and operators to select the GPU type, tensor-parallel degree, and precision before committing valuable node-hours. Making these choices is challenging because effective throughput, launch-success rates, and cluster demand and utilization continuously fluctuate. Furthermore, static configuration recipes miss critical interactions: quantization effects depend heavily on the model family, key-value cache pressure creates size-by-precision trade-offs, and failure rates vary by more than twofold across different tensor-parallel degrees. Additionally, cluster resources are frequently constrained by unpredictable hardware failures. To address these challenges, we present \textbf{OmniPilot}, a launch advisor that predicts serving costs for feasible configurations and abstains when requests fall outside its measured support envelope. OmniPilot pairs a conformally calibrated quantile cost model (spanning eight serving targets) with an out-of-distribution (OOD) abstention layer. It ranks configurations using an economic utility metric calibrated to an operator's revealed preferences. In evaluations across 460 benchmark runs on A100, H100, and H200 hardware across four precisions, OmniPilot predicts aggregate throughput with a 6.2\% mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) and a log-space $R^2=0.92$. The advisor achieves 95\% top-1 accuracy with a mean utility regret of just 0.003. When tested on an OOD holdout of unsupported cells, prediction error climbs to 24-46\% and conformal intervals cover 0 of 5 points; however, the abstention layer successfully flags all five as low-confidence. Over time, these OOD scenarios will be integrated into the training dataset to continuously expand the advisor's support envelope.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的全连接序列并行方法在处理中等长度序列时，通信和计算严格串行执行，导致硬件资源利用率不足。

Method: 利用多头注意力的计算独立性，将注意力头划分为多个块，通过双CUDA流实现细粒度的通信-计算重叠。支持不均匀划分，保持数值等价性，无需修改底层kernel。

Result: 在四种GPU平台2-8卡规模上，对31K-56K tokens的视频生成序列，相比Ulysses加速10%-17.5%，相比Ring Attention加速5%-14.5%；在Wan2.2模型上端到端加速6.8%。

Abstract: All-to-all based sequence parallelism methods execute communication and computation strictly in serial when processing medium-long sequences, resulting in hardware resource underutilization. This paper proposes Head-Chunked Multi-Stream Pipeline (HCMS), which exploits the computational independence of multi-head attention by partitioning attention heads into multiple chunks and achieving fine-grained communication-computation overlap through dual CUDA streams. HCMS is orthogonally compatible with existing optimizations such as FlashAttention and SDPA, requires no modification to underlying kernels, supports uneven partitioning while maintaining numerical equivalence. Experiments validate the effectiveness across four GPU platforms at 2-8 GPU scales: for typical video generation sequence lengths of 31K-56K tokens, HCMS achieves 10\%-17.5\% speedup over the Ulysses baseline and 5\%-14.5\% speedup over Ring Attention; end-to-end acceleration of 6.8\% is achieved on the Wan2.2 model. Theoretical analysis shows that HCMS benefits are positively correlated with communication ratio $ρ$, and its use is recommended when $ρ>20\%$.

### [12] [Lynx: Progressive Speculative Quantization for accelerating KV Transfer in Long-Context Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01831)
*Wenchen Han,Gingfung Matthew Yeung,Marco Barletta,William Toner,Amory Hoste,Adam Barker*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Lynx系统通过将KV缓存分割为高优先级Anchor流（含最高有效位）和低优先级Residual流（含剩余精度），实现渐进式分流传输。解码在接收Anchor流后即可开始，同时后台传输Residual流并验证结果，在保持高推理精度的同时显著降低首令牌延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文推理中KV缓存网络传输成为瓶颈，现有量化方案无法同时实现低延迟和高精度。作者挑战"KV缓存必须完整接收后才可使用"的假设，利用不同比特位对注意力计算贡献不均的特性。

Method: 将KV缓存按比特重要性分层：最高有效位组成Anchor流（捕获注意力粗略结构），剩余比特组成Residual流（细化精度）。解码时先接收Anchor流进行推测性解码，同时后台传输Residual流，最后验证以保证与高精度解码等价。

Result: TTFT与激进4-bit量化相当，精度匹配BF16推理；相比标准8-bit量化TTFT提升1.43倍，相比最先进方法精度提升5.1%。

Conclusion: 验证了KV缓存不必作为不可分割整体传输的思路，通过渐进式传输能在不牺牲精度的情况下大幅降低网络暴露延迟，为长上下文LLM推理优化提供了新范式。

Abstract: Long-context inference is increasingly common in large language model (LLM) serving, driven by retrieval-augmented generation and agentic systems. In disaggregated inference, these workloads require transferring large Key-Value (KV) caches across the network, where decoding cannot begin until the transfer completes. Recent KV quantization techniques reduce data volume and alleviate this bottleneck, but existing schemes fail to achieve both low network-exposed latency and high inference accuracy.
  We challenge the assumption that the KV cache is an indivisible unit that must be fully received before use. We leverage the observation that different bits in the KV cache contribute unequally to attention computation and inference precision: the most significant bits capture the coarse structure of attention and the least significant bits refine precision. This property enables partial use of the KV cache during decoding. We present Lynx, a system that enables progressive, split-stream KV transfer by partitioning the KV cache into a high-priority Anchor stream carrying the most significant bits and a low-priority Residual stream carrying remaining precision. Decoding begins upon receipt of the Anchor stream and proceeds speculatively while the Residual stream is transferred concurrently, followed by verification that ensures equivalence to higher-precision decoding.
  Across multiple models and serving workloads, Lynx achieves Time-to-First-Token (TTFT) comparable to aggressive 4-bit KV quantization, while matching the accuracy of high-precision (BF16) inference, improving TTFT over standard 8-bit KV quantization by up to $1.43\times$ and improving accuracy over state-of-the-art by up to $5.1\%$.

</details>

Abstract: This paper showcases a memory-efficient training stack for Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models. It leverages these techniques to achieve maximal efficiency given the physical constraints of CPU, CPU memory, GPU HBM memory, and the CPU-GPU, GPU-GPU, and node-node communication bandwidth of the GPU cluster. ### [14] [Towards Load-Aware Prefill Deflection for Disaggregated LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02043)
*Shrikara Arun,Anjaly Parayil,Srikant Bharadwaj,Renee St. Amant,Victor Rühle*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了一种主动式预填充偏转调度器（proactive prefill-deflecting scheduler），允许解码节点以分块预填充步骤（chunked-prefill steps）的方式服务于请求的预填充阶段，与正在进行的解码批次交错执行，从而消除排队和跨节点KV缓存传输导致的TTFT延迟问题，在A100 2P2D集群上将P95 TTFT降低高达81%，SLO达成率提升高达79%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分离式LLM服务中，预填充节点在突发性重尾工作负载下容易饱和，而解码节点计算资源利用不足。预填充执行仅占P95 TTFT的2-23%，其余大部分时间浪费在排队和跨节点GPU-GPU KV缓存传输上，亟需解决这一不对称问题。

Method: 提出主动式预填充偏转调度器，核心思路是：1) 解码节点以分块预填充步骤（chunked-prefill steps）形式处理被偏转请求的预填充阶段，与解码批次交错执行；2) 对每个排队请求，分别估算其在预填充节点和各解码节点上的TTFT；3) 在解码节点上搜索最大分块调度方案，确保不影响正在处理的解码请求的TBT SLO；4) 当解码路径有助于改善尾部延迟时，将请求偏转到解码节点处理，同时消除跨节点KV传输。

Result: 在vLLM上实现，使用DeepSeek-V2-Lite模型和生产线级trace进行评估，相比最先进的分离式调度器，P95 TTFT降低高达81%，SLO达成率提升高达79%，每个请求的路由开销在亚毫秒级别。

Conclusion: 通过让解码节点主动承接预填充任务，有效缓解了分离式架构中预填充节点过载而解码节点空闲的不对称问题，显著降低了尾部TTFT延迟，同时保持了极低的路由开销。

Abstract: Disaggregated LLM serving runs prefill and decode on separate GPU pools to keep the two phases from interfering. In practice, this creates a new asymmetry: under bursty, heavy-tailed workloads prefill nodes saturate while decode nodes have compute underutilized, and on a production-style A100 cluster with 2 prefill and 2 decode nodes (2P2D), we find that prefill execution accounts for only 2-23% of P95 Time-to-First-Token (TTFT). Queuing and inter-node GPU-GPU KV-cache transfer account for the rest. We present a proactive prefill-deflecting scheduler that lets decode nodes serve prefill phase of requests as chunked-prefill steps interleaved with their in-flight decode batches. For each queued request, we estimate the TTFT it would see on the prefill node, and on every decode node, search for the largest chunk schedule that keeps in-flight decodes within their Time-Between-Tokens (TBT) SLO and deflect when the decode path helps tail latency. Because the prefill phase of deflected requests runs in place on the decode node, the inter-node KV transfer is eliminated. Implemented on vLLM and evaluated on production-style traces with DeepSeek-V2-Lite, our approach reduces P95 TTFT by upto 81% and raises SLO attainment by upto 79% over state-of-the-art disaggregated schedulers, at sub-millisecond per-request routing cost.

### [15] [Cadence: Extreme Pipelining with Multiple Concurrent Proposers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02275)
*Fatima Elsheimy,Mohammad Mussadiq Jalalzai,Tobias Klenze,Jovan Komatovic,Mike Setrin,Victor Shoup,Kushal Babel,Lioba Heimbach,Jason Milionis*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: Cadence 是一种拜占庭容错的多提案者共识协议，支持极低区块间隔、最优容错性和最优快速路径延迟。它通过"极端流水线"将区块间隔与网络延迟解耦，并实现多并发提案者下的短期抗审查性和隐藏性，在 Monad 模拟中平均最终确认时间为 219ms。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共识协议存在两个核心问题：1) 区块间隔受限于网络延迟，传统流水线方式中后一个区块需等待前一个区块完成；2) 单一领导者垄断交易的包含和排序权，导致审查风险和排序不公。Cadence 旨在解耦区块间隔与网络延迟，并实现多提案者下的抗审查性和隐藏性。

Method: Cadence 将时间划分为等距时隙，每个时隙独立运行一个共识实例，区块不直接依赖前驱，实现"极端流水线"。引入通用框架将任意单次共识（slot-consensus）转化为多次协议。提出 Chorus（三回合快速路径最终确认，一轮即可推测性最终确认）和 Conductor（以均匀节奏开启时隙，异步下放缓速度以控制开放时隙数量）两个子协议。

Result: 在 Monad 200 个验证者、每时隙 5 个提案者的模拟中，最终确认平均 219ms（推测性最终确认 167ms）；在 100ms 区块间隔下，交易平均等待 50ms 进入提案。证明了在部分同步模型下安全、活性、抗审查性和隐藏性，达到最优容错 n=3f+1。

Conclusion: Cadence 是首个在单领导者共识快速路径延迟下实现短期抗审查性和隐藏性的多并发提案者协议，通过极端流水线有效解耦区块间隔与网络延迟。

Abstract: We present Cadence, a Byzantine fault-tolerant multi-proposer consensus protocol with arbitrarily low block intervals, optimal resilience, and optimal fast-path latency. Cadence divides time into equally spaced slots, one block per slot, each finalized in its own consensus instance. Blocks do not build directly on their predecessor, so instances run independently and none waits for an earlier block to finish or propagate; we call this extreme pipelining, decoupling the block interval from network latency. Cadence also removes the single-leader monopoly over transaction inclusion and ordering: under multiple concurrent proposers (MCP), several validators propose for each block, and it guarantees that, under synchrony, a transaction a correct proposer includes cannot be censored or deferred (short-term censorship resistance), and that no proposer can craft its proposal in reaction to the others' (hiding). To realize extreme pipelining, we introduce a general framework that turns any one-shot consensus meeting our slot-consensus specification into a multi-shot protocol. We instantiate it for MCP with two protocols of our own: Chorus, a slot consensus whose fast path finalizes a block in an optimal three rounds, with speculative finality one round earlier, and Conductor, an orchestrator that opens slots at an even cadence, more slowly under asynchrony to keep open slots bounded. To our knowledge, Cadence is the first MCP protocol to provide short-term censorship resistance and hiding at the fast-path latency of single-leader consensus. We prove safety, liveness, censorship resistance, and hiding under partial synchrony with optimal resilience (n = 3f+1). In simulation over Monad's 200 validators with five proposers per slot, finalization averages 219 ms (167 ms to speculative finality); at a 100 ms block interval a transaction waits on average 50 ms to enter a proposal.

</details>


### [16] [Securing People and their Machines Against Major Faults](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02304)
*Ohad Eitan,Idit Keidar,Ehud Shapiro*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对草根平台的去中心化恢复机制，通过社交图、身份托管人和状态托管人，在用户丢失私钥或智能手机时实现安全恢复，并保证了规范与实现的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 草根平台缺乏全局资源支持，当用户丢失私钥或智能手机时，无法依赖中心化服务进行恢复，因此需要去中心化的对等解决方案来保障系统安全。

Method: 基于草根社交图、身份托管人和状态托管人，通过超级多数同意机制实现公钥替换和友谊恢复；使用受保护的多智能体原子事务进行规范描述，并通过通信的自愿智能体在最终同步消息传递模型中实现。

Result: 证明了实现模型中的可恢复故障运行与规范中的正确运行之间的映射关系；对草根货币和债券也实现了类似的状态恢复，包括单写入者日志的精确恢复和主权恢复后的防双花。

Conclusion: 该方案为去中心化身份和状态恢复提供了形式化保证，并为草根平台的安全性与可靠性奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider grassroots platforms -- distributed systems of agents consisting of people identified by self-chosen public keys and their machines (smartphones) -- and wish to make them secure against \emph{major faults}: the loss of their private keys and/or their smartphones. As grassroots platforms have no global resource to rely on for recovery, our peer-based solution is based on: (\ia) \emph{a grassroots social graph} in which agents establish and maintain friendships; (\ib) \emph{identity custodians}, designated by each person, and (\ic) \emph{state custodians}, which are grassroots platform-specific. Upon a person experiencing identity loss, and given a willing supermajority of the identity custodians of the person, the friends of the person replace the old public key with the new one across the graph and restore friendships, where all friends serve as state custodians for the social graph. Choosing a new keypair, obtaining a new smartphone, and convincing identity custodians to will a change of key all happen ``off-chain''. Recovery from machine loss without loss of key (e.g. smartphone run over by truck, or its memory wiped) is simpler, requiring only the help of state custodians.
  We specify the social graph and its secure version as guarded multiagent atomic transactions, and implement the secure social graph via communicating volitional agents, an eventually synchronous message-passing model one step closer to implementation. We prove the implementation maps runs with recoverable faults to correct runs of the specification.
  We follow a similar path for grassroots coins and bonds, showing a common core as well as the platform-specific aspects of state recovery: a currency's single-writer log is recovered exactly, the recovered sovereign resuming without double-spending.

</details>


### [17] [Elasticity in Parallel Sparse Triangular Solve](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02324)
*Raphael S. Steiner,Christos K. Matzoros,Pál András Papp,Toni Böhnlein,A. N. Yzelman*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的同步并行调度器在稀疏三角线性系统求解中由于同步开销限制了性能，需要探索新的执行模式来重叠同步与计算以提升并行效率。

Method: 提出陈旧同步并行（SSP）执行模式，并设计一个通用的DAG调度器ElasticDivide，该调度器能够产生SSP调度，允许同步操作与计算任务重叠执行。

Result: 在ARM机器（48核）上，ElasticDivide相比最先进的同步调度器GrowLocal获得7-30%的几何平均加速；在x86机器（48核）上，相比SpMP获得19-60%的几何平均加速。

Conclusion: 陈旧同步并行模式能有效提升稀疏三角线性系统求解的并行性能，所提出的ElasticDivide调度器在多种架构上均优于现有的同步调度方法。

Abstract: We introduce stale synchronous parallel as a mode of execution in parallel sparse triangular linear system solve and present a general directed-acyclic-graph scheduler capable of producing such schedules. Stale-synchronous-parallel schedules allow the overlap of synchronisation and compute which results in a geometric-mean speed-up of $7$-$30\%$ of our scheduler, ElasticDivide, over state-of-the-art synchronous scheduler GrowLocal on an ARM machine using 48 cores. On an x86 machine using 48 cores, we report geometric-mean speed-ups of $19$-$60\%$ over SpMP.

### [18] [WattGPU: Predicting Inference Power and Latency on Unseen GPUs and LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02391)
*Mauricio Fadel Argerich,Jonathan Fürst,Marta Patiño-Martínez*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出WattGPU，一种仅利用公开的LLM元数据和GPU规格即可预测GPU功耗和推理延迟的预测模型，无需硬件访问或性能剖析，在未见过的GPU和LLM上实现了高精度（功耗误差≤3.4%/13.5%，延迟误差≤8.5%），相比传统基线方法误差降低约2-4倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM推理工作负载快速增长导致数据中心能耗激增，但运维人员缺乏高效工具来为特定LLM匹配最节能GPU。现有预测模型仍需性能剖析数据，且难以泛化到训练中未见过的硬件。

Method: 构建两个预测模型分别预测GPU平均功耗和Token间延迟（ITL）。仅依赖LLM公开元数据和GPU规格参数，无需实际硬件访问。使用留一GPU和留一LLM交叉验证，在42个开源LLM（0.1B-27B参数）和8种GPU上评估离线与服务器两种场景。

Result: 功耗模型在未见过的GPU上中位绝对百分比误差：离线场景≤3.4%，服务器场景≤13.5%。延迟模型在服务器场景≤8.5%。GPU排名相关性Kendall τ≥0.76。相比基于TDP和roofline的基线方法，误差降低约2-4倍。

Conclusion: WattGPU展示了无需硬件剖析即可高精度预测LLM推理功耗和延迟的可行性，为数据中心节能优化提供了实用的工具，代码和数据已开源。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) inference workloads are a rapidly growing contributor to data center energy consumption. Optimizing these deployments requires matching specific LLMs to the most efficient GPUs, but operators currently lack the tools to do so without exhaustively profiling each combination. While some predictive models exist, they still require profiling data and struggle to generalize to hardware unseen during training. To address this, we introduce \textit{WattGPU}, featuring two predictive models for mean GPU power draw and Inter-Token Latency (ITL). Our approach leverages only publicly available LLM metadata and GPU specifications, eliminating the need for hardware access or profiling while enabling generalization to unseen NVIDIA server-grade GPUs and LLMs. We evaluate our models using rigorous leave-one-GPU-out and leave-one-LLM-out cross-validation on a dataset of 42 open-source LLMs (0.1B--27B parameters) and 8 GPUs under both offline and server scenarios. The mean power draw model achieves a median absolute percentage error of $\leq3.4\%$ for offline and $\leq13.5\%$ for server scenarios on unseen GPUs, while the latency model achieves $\leq8.5\%$ in server mode, both maintaining strong GPU ranking correlations for server scenarios (Kendall $τ\geq0.76$). Compared to standard physically grounded baselines -- Load-Scaled Thermal Design Power (TDP) for power draw and roofline for latency -- our models reduce median absolute percentage error by approximately 4$\times$ on unseen LLM-GPU combinations for server scenarios or approximately 2$\times$ for completely unseen GPUs. WattGPU's data and code are publicly available at https://github.com/maufadel/wattgpu.

### [19] [FlintKV: A Fast Durable Storage Engine for Modern Databases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02401)
*Sergey Egorov,Gregory Chockler,Brijesh Dongol,Dan O'Keeffe,Sadegh Keshavarzi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: FlintKV 是一种基于 NVM 优化的跳表存储引擎，支持生产级键值存储的完整 API（原子批处理、快照一致性迭代、持久化线性一致性），通过新型扁平合并并发控制和多版本机制，实现了比现有方案最高 75% 的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 NVM 键值存储虽然在高吞吐量摄取和点查询上表现良好，但缺乏对现代数据库所需的事务支持（如快照、一致性迭代、原子批处理），无法满足生产级存储引擎的接口要求。

Method: FlintKV 提出了一种基于扁平合并（flat-combining）的并发控制算法，结合多版本控制和精心设计的持久化机制，构建了 NVM 优化的跳表存储引擎，原生支持原子批写入和快照一致性迭代。

Result: 实验表明，FlintKV 在端到端吞吐量上比现有方案提升了最高 75%。

Conclusion: FlintKV 证明了通过协同设计并发控制与持久化机制，可以在 NVM 上实现兼具高性能与丰富语义的生产级存储引擎。

Abstract: Byte-addressable non-volatile memory (NVM) offers an opportunity to rethink storage engine architectures. While recent NVM key-value stores achieve high throughput for ingestion and point lookups, they omit or under-specify the support for the richer interface guarantees required by modern databases. Production key-value engines (e.g., RocksDB) provide point-in-time snapshots, consistent iterators, and atomic batches-features essential for implementing transactions and concurrency control. We present FlintKV, an NVM-optimized skiplist-based storage engine that natively supports the full API of production key-value stores. FlintKV supports both atomic batch writes and snapshot-consistent iteration efficiently while guaranteeing durable linearizability. FlintKV can be deployed standalone or its durable skiplist can be integrated into existing NVM stores to enhance their capabilities. Central to FlintKV is a novel flat-combining based concurrency control algorithm that leverages multi-versioning and carefully co-designed persistence mechanisms to ensure high performance and scalability. Our empirical evaluation shows that FlintKV can achieve up to a 75% improvement in end-to-end throughput over prior work.

</details>

### [20] [Robustifying Sparse Matrix Multiplication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01427)
*Karl Bringmann,Nick Fischer,Vasileios Nakos*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出一个黑盒约简方法，能将任意稀疏矩阵乘法算法转化为鲁棒版本（可近似计算k个最大输出项），仅需多对数开销，并通过集成最新算法实现了接近最优的复杂度上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有稀疏矩阵乘法算法几乎都不具备鲁棒性（即近似误差仅依赖于较小项），唯一例外是Pagh算法。作者希望探寻能否将其他算法也转化为鲁棒形式。

Method: 提出黑盒约简：将鲁棒稀疏矩阵乘法问题转化为常规稀疏矩阵乘法问题，仅增加多对数开销。该约简利用稀疏恢复工具，并涉及求解背包类型问题。具体而言，若常规算法时间复杂度为T(n, m_in, m_out)，则鲁棒版本时间复杂度为Õ(T(n, m_in, k))。

Result: 将最新稀疏矩阵乘法算法（Abboud等人，SODA'24）代入该框架，得到O((m_in + k)^{1.346})的鲁棒算法。当k ≥ m_in^{1.762}时，进一步达到接近最优的k^{1+o(1)}时间复杂度。

Conclusion: 本文首次系统性地将非鲁棒的稀疏矩阵乘法算法转化为鲁棒版本，填补了该领域的重要空白，并为后续研究提供了通用框架。

Abstract: In the seminal sparse matrix multiplication problem the goal is to compute the product of two $n \times n$ matrices when the matrices are sparse, i.e., when the number of nonzeros in the input matrices $m_{in}$ and/or the number of nonzeros in the output matrix $m_{out}$ are much smaller than $n^2$. In this paper, we explore the generalized problem of (approximately) computing the $k$ largest output entries, with an approximation error dependent solely on the smaller entries -- from the viewpoint of sparse recovery, this can be seen as a robust variant of sparse matrix multiplication. Despite the substantial research dedicated to sparse matrix multiplication, almost no existing algorithms are robust in this sense. The one exception is Pagh's algorithm in time $\widetilde O(m_{in} + nk)$ [ITCS'12], and it remained open whether other algorithms can be similarly made robust.
  Our principal contribution is a black-box reduction from robust sparse matrix multiplication to conventional sparse matrix multiplication with only polylogarithmic overhead. Specifically, we show that any sparse matrix multiplication algorithm with running time $T(n, m_{in}, m_{out})$ can be transformed into a robust algorithm running in time $\widetilde O(T(n, m_{in}, k))$. This reduction leverages an extensive toolkit from sparse recovery, and intriguingly, also involves solving a knapsack-type problem.
  By plugging in the state-of-the-art algorithm for sparse matrix multiplication by Abboud, Bringmann, Fischer, and Künnemann [SODA'24], we achieve significantly improved bounds such as $O((m_{in} + k)^{1.346})$. Notably, in the regime where $k \geq m_{in}^{1.762}$, our reduction culminates in an almost-optimal $k^{1+o(1)}$-time algorithm.

</details>


### [21] [Asymmetric Trading Prophets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01516)
*Gagan Aggarwal,Anupam Gupta,Yifan Wang,Mingfei Zhao*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究非对称交易先知问题，其中每时间步买卖价格不同且可任意相关。针对不同容量和初始库存，设计了在线算法并证明了竞争比，在对称情形下逼近最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交易先知问题假设买卖价格相同，无法捕捉去中心化市场中买卖机会分离的结构性不对称性。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 针对容量B=1情形，对i.i.d.和非i.i.d.分布设计常数竞争比算法；对一般容量B，对i.i.d.分布设计竞争比为1 - Θ(log B₀/√B₀)的算法；对称情形下改进至1 - O(log B/√B)。

Result: 在单位容量且有一份初始库存时，i.i.d.和非i.i.d.情形均实现常数竞争比；一般容量下竞争比达1 - Θ(log B₀/√B₀)；对称情形下改进至1 - O(log B/√B)，且证明紧性至对数因子。

Conclusion: 非对称交易先知问题可刻画去中心化市场的买卖分离特性，所提算法随容量增大趋近最优，且竞争比界在理论上是紧的。

Abstract: The "Trading Prophet" problem challenges an online trader to maximize its profit by buying and selling assets under stochastic prices and capacity constraints, competing against an offline prophet with full foresight. In previous work, each arriving asset was assumed to have a single price $p_t$, and the trader was allowed to either buy a copy at this price (subject to having available capacity), or sell a copy (if it already held at least one copy in hand). However, this abstraction can fail to capture the structural asymmetry of decentralized dealer-based markets, where buying and selling opportunities could be distinct, and driven by individual preferences. To address this, we introduce the Asymmetric Trading Prophets problem, where at each timestep the trader observes a price tuple $(b_t, s_t)$ -- representing the cost to buy, and the revenue from selling at this timestep. Importantly, the $(b_t,s_t)$ tuple could be potentially arbitrarily correlated.
  We provide the first competitive analysis for this asymmetric trading prophets problem, characterizing the achievable profit based on the trader's capacity $B$ and initial inventory $B_0$. For the unit-capacity case of $B=1$, we design online algorithms that achieve constant competitive ratios for both i.i.d. and non-i.i.d. distributions on the price tuples, when the trader has one initial copy ($B_0=1$). For the general capacity case where $B$ can be large, we give algorithms for i.i.d. distributions that achieve a competitive ratio of $1 - Θ(\log B_0/\sqrt{B_0})$. Finally, for the symmetric case (where the price tuple satisfies $b_t=s_t$), we improve this to get a competitive ratio of $1 - O(\log B/\sqrt{B})$, demonstrating that the performance approaches optimality as the capacity increases. We show that both ratios are tight up to a logarithmic factor.

</details>


### [22] [Maximum Entropy is a 10/7-Approximation Algorithm for the TSP on Half-Integral Cycle Cut Instances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01536)
*Billy Jin,Nathan Klein,David P. Williamson*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对TSP问题中著名的三分之四猜想，证明了最大熵算法在半整数环割实例上能达到10/7近似比。虽然该结果并未改进整体积分间隙上界，但为其他实例类别的分析提供了方向和希望。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TSP的Subtour LP松弛的积分间隙（四分之三猜想）是组合优化中著名的开放问题，已有40年未取得本质突破。作者希望通过对特定实例类（半整数环割实例）的分析，为最终解决该猜想提供线索。

Method: 论文聚焦于半整数环割（half-integral cycle cut）实例这一特定类别，应用最大熵算法（max entropy algorithm）进行分析，并证明在该类实例上算法能达到10/7的近似比。

Result: 最大熵算法在半整数环割实例上的近似比为10/7。该类实例包含了积分间隙至少为4/3的示例，也包含表明最大熵算法性能不超过11/8的示例。但作者指出，已有最新工作证明了该类实例的积分间隙上界为4/3，因此本文并未（也不可能）改进整体积分间隙上界。

Conclusion: 尽管未直接改进四分之三猜想的上界，但本文表明最大熵算法在特定实例类上优于已知的一般上界（1.5），这说明一般实例的分析可能不是紧的，为后续改进整体分析提供了方向和希望。

Abstract: One of the most famous conjectures in combinatorial optimization is the four-thirds conjecture, which states that the integrality gap of the Subtour LP relaxation of the TSP is equal to $\frac{4}{3}$. For 40 years, the best known upper bound was $1.5$, due to Wolsey. Recently, Karlin, Klein, and Oveis Gharan showed that the max entropy algorithm for the TSP gives an improved bound of $1.5 - 10^{-36}$. In this paper, we show that the maximum entropy algorithm is a $\frac{10}{7}$-approximation for half-integral cycle cut instances of the TSP. This class of instances contains examples which demonstrate the subtour LP has an integrality gap of at least $\frac{4}{3}$, as well as examples showing that the performance of the max entropy algorithm is no better than $\frac{11}{8}$. We note that in the authors recently gave an algorithm upper bounding the integrality gap of this class of instances by $\frac{4}{3}$, so this work does not (and could not) provide an improved bound on the integrality gap. However, since there is no reason to believe that the analysis of the maximum entropy algorithm on general instances is tight, our work provides hope (and potentially direction) for improved analysis on other instance classes.

</details>


### [23] [Testing Unate Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01573)
*Daeho Lee,Shivam Nadimpalli,Mingda Qiao,Ronitt Rubinfeld*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文首次研究 $\{\pm1\}^n$ 上的单峰分布，证明均匀性测试需要 $\widetildeΘ(n^{3/2})$ 样本（对比单调分布的 $\widetildeΘ(n)$），并给出子立方条件模型下单峰性测试的 $\widetilde{O}(n^{3/2})$ 算法及 $\widetildeΩ(n^{2/3})$ 下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将单调布尔函数的"单峰性"概念推广到概率分布，系统研究单峰分布的测试问题，填补该方向的空白。

Method: 提出"弱学习"单峰分布隐藏方向的子程序，结合新的相关性界估计；在子立方条件模型下设计测试器，并与单调性测试进行对比分析。

Result: 均匀性测试：$\widetildeΘ(n^{3/2})$ 样本复杂度（紧界）；单峰性测试：$\widetilde{O}(n^{3/2})$ 上界，$\widetildeΩ(n^{2/3})$ 下界（$O(1)$-维子立方情形）。

Conclusion: 单峰分布的测试复杂度显著高于单调分布，但比朴素归约方法（$Ω(n^2)$）有指数级改进；所提工具可独立应用于其他单调性/单峰性研究。

Abstract: We initiate the study of *unate distributions* over $\{\pm1\}^n$ -- a natural analogue of unate Boolean functions -- by considering two basic testing problems that parallel well-studied questions for monotone distributions:
  - Uniformity Testing of Unate Distributions: We show that $\widetildeΘ(n^{3/2})$ samples are sufficient and necessary, in contrast to the $\widetildeΘ(n)$ sample complexity of the analogous problem for monotone distributions (Rubinfeld and Servedio, STOC 2005; Adamaszek, Czumaj, and Sohler, SODA 2010).
  - Unateness Testing of Arbitrary Distributions: We give a tester that uses $\widetilde{O}(n^{3/2})$ conditional samples in the subcube conditional model. On the other hand, every tester that draws conditional samples in a similar fashion, namely from $O(1)$-dimensional subcubes, must have an $\widetildeΩ(n^{2/3})$ complexity. In the same model, the complexity of monotonicity testing was recently shown to be $\widetildeΘ(n)$ (Chakrabarty et al., STOC 2025).
  Our algorithms for both problems significantly outperform the naive approach of reducing to the monotone case, which would incur $Ω(n^2)$ sample complexity. Our uniformity tester relies on a subroutine that "weakly" learns the hidden orientations of a unate distribution, together with a new correlation bound for these estimates. Both tools may be of independent interest in studying monotonicity and unateness over $\{\pm1\}^n$.

</details>


### [24] [Fully Persistent Dynamic LCE via AVL Trees and AVL Grammars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01580)
*Taiki Kaneda,Hiroki Arimura,Shunsuke Inenaga*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于AVL树的完全持久化动态字符串结构FeAVL，支持分裂、拼接、单字符更新（最坏情况O(log n)）、相等性查询（最坏情况O(log n) w.h.p.）和最长公共扩展LCE查询（最坏情况O(log n + log²ℓ) w.h.p.），每次更新仅创建O(log n)个新永久节点。此外还给出了基于AVL文法的压缩实例化方案，有效控制永久文法节点的增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对splay-based FeST结构在完全持久化场景下因旧版本被无限重用而导致平摊分析失效的问题，需要一种能够在完全持久化环境下依然保证高效性能的动态字符串结构。

Method: 采用基于AVL树的路径复制（path copying）策略实现完全持久化，设计了FeAVL结构。对于压缩场景，引入AVL文法（AVL grammars）进行文法压缩实例化。

Result: FeAVL支持分裂、拼接、单字符更新在最坏情况O(log n)时间内完成；相等性查询在最坏情况O(log n)时间（高概率）；LCE查询在最坏情况O(log n + log²ℓ)时间（高概率）。每次更新仅产生O(log n)个新永久节点。压缩版本中，经过U次更新后，永久文法节点总数为O(g₀ + I + U log n_max)。

Conclusion: 提出了一种在完全持久化设定下高效且优雅的动态字符串结构FeAVL，解决了现有结构在持久化环境下的局限性，同时在压缩场景下也具有良好的空间效率。

Abstract: We study fully persistent dynamic strings with equality and longest common extension (LCE) queries. Straightforward full persistence is problematic for the splay-based FeST structure, since the same unbalanced past version can be reused indefinitely and the usual amortized analysis no longer applies. We give a fully persistent dynamic LCE structure, called FeAVL, based on path copying over AVL trees. For an operation involving string(s) of total length $n$, it supports split, concatenate, and single-character updates in worst-case $O(\log n)$ time, equality in worst-case $O(\log n)$ time w.h.p., and LCE in worst-case $O(\log n+\log^2\ell)$ time w.h.p., where $\ell$ is the answer; each update creates only $O(\log n)$ new permanent nodes. We also give a grammar-compressed instantiation via AVL grammars: starting from an initial grammar of size $g_0$, after $U$ updates, the total number of permanent grammar nodes is $O(g_0+I+U\log n_{\max})$, where $I$ is the number of inserted fresh characters and $n_{\max}$ is the maximum string length appearing during the update sequence.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过图灵归约，将 Telephone Broadcast 问题转化为带权 b-匹配问题，从而设计出更高效的参数化算法。

Abstract: Given a connected graph $G$ and a source $s \in V(G)$, what is the smallest number of rounds necessary for all vertices of $G$ to receive a message initially only held by $s$, where at each round every informed vertex passes the message to one of its neighbors? This problem is called Telephone Broadcast and is suprisingly hard: it remains NP-hard on cycles intersecting at a single shared vertex, in particular, graphs of pathwidth 2 with a linear feedback vertex set of size 1, as well as on graphs with treedepth at most 6 [Egami et al.; MFCS '25]. Vertex cover number, vertex integrity, and distance to clique are among the few parameters for which Telephone Broadcast is fixed-parameter tractable. There is a $2^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^3)} n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$-time algorithm parameterized by vertex cover number $\mathrm{vc}$ [Fomin, Fraigniaud, Golovach; TCS '24], a double-exponential algorithm parameterized by vertex integrity $\mathrm{vi}$, and a $2^{\mathcal{O}(k^2)} n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$-time algorithm parameterized by distance to clique $k$ [Egami et al.; MFCS '25].
  In this paper, we give improved parameterized algorithms for Telephone Broadcast with running times $2^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc} \log \mathrm{vc})} n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$, $2^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vi}^2 \log \mathrm{vi})} n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$, and $2^{\mathcal{O}(k \log k)} n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$. The main ingredient that makes our algorithms faster is a Turing reduction to edge-weighted $b$-Matching.

Surprisingly, existing approximate methods using $O(n^2)$ distance calculations are heuristics not offering provable and controllable guarantees on the quality of their results.

Our distributed algorithms use a constant number of rounds and sublinear local memory. Finally, we perform extensive experiments against state-of-the-art approaches. The results show that our new techniques yield the best trade-off between accuracy and efficiency for both local and global silhouette estimation. ### [30] [Fine-Grained Bounds for Courcelle's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02033)

TL;DR: 本文提出了Courcelle定理的细粒度版本，在树宽参数t和公式φ的量词结构上实现了接近ETH紧致的依赖关系。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Courcelle定理上下界之间存在巨大差距（如单指数与双指数运行时间差异），且对时间复杂度的理解过于粗糙，需要更精确的刻画。

Method: 通过精细分析MSO公式中每个量词交替块内一阶和二阶变量的数量，建立与树宽参数t的紧致依赖关系。

Abstract: Courcelle's theorem states that there exists an algorithm that takes as input a graph $G$ of treewidth at most $t$ and a MSO formula $φ$, and determines whether $G$ satisfies $φ$ in time $f(φ,t) \cdot n$. It is folklore that the the function $f$ contains a tower of exponentials whose height depends as a linear function of the number of quantifier alternations of the input formula $φ$. A classic reduction of Frick and Grohe shows that, assuming the Exponential Time Hypothesis (ETH), the linear growth of the height of the tower is unavoidable. Nevertheless, there is still a huge gap between existing upper and lower bounds -- after all, there is quite a difference between a single exponential and a double exponential running time. In addition, this only gives us a very coarse understanding in the time complexity of Courcelle's theorem. In this paper, we prove a fine-grained version of Courcelle's theorem with nearly ETH-tight dependence on the treewidth parameter $t$ and the quantifier structure of $φ$ (specifically, the number of first order and second order variables in each quantifier alternation block).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Pattern matching on strings is regarded as one of the core operations in computer science. Although researchers proposed several solutions to this problem, some of the most elegant and widely used approaches are based on the renowned Burrows-Wheeler transform (BWT). The success of the BWT lies in its pattern matching algorithm known as backward search, which is not only near-optimal in the RAM model, but also runs directly on a compressed representation of the input string. More recently, the backward search has been generalized to Wheeler deterministic finite automata (DFAs), a subclass of standard DFAs, without losing its near-optimal time efficiency. Similarly to the case of strings, this pattern matching algorithm for Wheeler DFAs has found applications in bioinformatics, where researchers have shown that specific pangenome graphs of human chromosomes can be transformed into Wheeler DFAs and consequently indexed using this strategy. However, this BWT-based index on Wheeler DFAs inherited a significant drawback from the original backward search, namely the high number of I/O operations triggered during the algorithm execution, which are in the worst-case lower-bounded by the length of the pattern. In this paper, we address this limitation by proposing the first cache-friendly algorithm specifically designed for Wheeler DFAs. Our new data structure reduces the number of I/O operations by employing a strategy analogous to the suffix array: it interleaves a binary search with fast sequential scans of the automaton. We empirically validate this new indexing strategy by running our algorithm on real-world Wheeler pangenome graphs. We show that while our data structure can use up to 15 times the space required by the backward search, it can also be 500 times faster and able to process a single character of the pattern in less than 3 ns.

Abstract: This paper studies additive regret in the multi-secretary problem, defined as the gap between the expected offline prophet reward and the reward of the best online policy. Prior work established \(O(\log T)\) regret for bounded-density distributions with connected support and \(O((\log T)^2)\) upper bounds for bounded-density distributions with support gaps. It was unknown whether the extra logarithmic factor is necessary even in the one-resource model. We prove that it is necessary. For a mixture of two separated uniform distributions at the critical capacity, the optimal regret grows at least on the order of \((\log T)^2\). Thus the existing \(O((\log T)^2)\) upper bounds for bounded-density gapped instances, including those implied by network revenue management models with continuous rewards, are tight in this simplest specialization. The same framework also yields a matching lower bound for gapped distributions whose gap-facing densities vanish near the support edges; this companion result is given in the appendix. The proofs use Bellman certificates: feasible solutions to a relaxation of the exact Bellman recursion. This framework converts lower bounds into explicit certificate constructions and identifies why support gaps permit larger regret.

### [33] [Deterministic Polynomial-time Exact-root Computation for Sparse Polynomials with Bounded Total Degree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02364)
*Qiao-Long Huang,Yichuan Cao,Ruichen Qiu,Xiao-Shan Gao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多元多项式分解中，计算精确 e 次方根是一个基本问题。已有的确定性分解算法（如 Bhargava 等人）仅达到拟多项式复杂度，本文希望在总度数有界的场景下实现真正的多项式时间算法。

Method: 首先证明了基多项式 g 的稀疏度上界：‖g‖₀ ≤ s^{D(2d+2)/e + 1}。然后基于该界设计了一个确定性算法，复杂度为 poly(s^{O(Dd)}, n, d, D) + s·R(e)，其中 R(e) 是域上计算 e 次根或 Frobenius 根的成本。

Result: 证明了基多项式稀疏度的上界；在总度数 D 有界时，算法复杂度为多项式时间；在有限域、Q 或数域上，R(e) 项可被吸收进多项式复杂度界中。

Abstract: We study the problem of deterministically computing the exact root of a sparse polynomial in the multivariate setting. Let $f \in \F[x_1,\ldots,x_n]$ be a nonzero polynomial that is an exact $e$-th power, say $f = g^e$. Suppose $f$ is $s$-sparse, has an individual degree of at most $d$, and a total degree of $D = \tdeg(f)$. We prove a sparsity bound on the base polynomial $g$: \[ \|g\|_0 \le s^{D(2d+2)/e + 1}. \] Based on this bound, we develop a deterministic algorithm that computes the base $g$. %
In contrast to the general deterministic factorization algorithm of Bhargava, Saraf, and Volkovich \cite{BhargavaSarafVolkovich2020}, which achieves only a quasi-polynomial dependence on the input parameters, our algorithm is \emph{polynomial-time} in the setting where the total degree $D$ is bounded. Specifically, the overall complexity is \[ \mathrm{poly}\left(s^{O(Dd)}, n, d, D\right) + s\cdot R(e), \] %
where $R(e)$ denotes the cost of constructing a single $e$-th root of a scalar in the base field $\F$, and, when $\operatorname{char}(\F)\mid e$, the cost of computing a single Frobenius root of a scalar. %
This term is field-dependent, and over finite fields, $\mathbb{Q}$, or number fields with a suitable representation, it is absorbed into the polynomial complexity bound. %
Within the bounded total-degree regime, this yields a deterministic polynomial-time algorithm for exact-root computation.

</details>


### [34] [Improved Approximation Algorithms for n-Pairs Shortest Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02443)
*Avi Kadria,Liam Roditty,Virginia Vassilevska Williams*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对加权无向图中的 n-Pairs 最短路径问题，提出了首个达到 (2-α)k-近似且运行时间为 Õ(mn^{1/k} + n^{1+2/k}) 的算法，具体实现了 1.622k-近似，优于先前 (2k-3)-近似的结果，并回答了 Chechik 等人的开放问题。核心技术创新是“重边技术”（heavy-edge technique），将依赖于最重边权重的近似算法转化为纯乘法近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: n-Pairs 最短路径问题自 Cohen 提出后近年受到重新关注，现有算法在加权图上存在近似比与运行时间的 tradeoff 瓶颈。Chechik 等人 [SODA'25] 提出了 (2k-3)-近似算法，但留下了能否实现更好近似比的开放问题。本文旨在设计更优近似比的算法，并回答该开放问题。

Method: 提出“重边技术”（heavy-edge technique），将原本近似比依赖于路径上最重边权重 W_{uv} 的算法，转化为不依赖 W_{uv} 的纯乘法近似算法。利用该技术构造了加权无向图上的 n-Pairs 最短路径算法，实现了 (2-α)k-近似（常数 α>0），具体为 1.622k-近似，运行时间为 Õ(mn^{1/k} + n^{1+2/k})。同时针对无权重图和稠密加权图给出了改进的近似算法。

Result: 首次在加权无向图上实现了 (2-α)k-近似，具体达到 1.622k-近似，改进了 Chechik 等人 (2k-3)-近似的结果。在无权重图和稠密加权图上进一步改进了 Dalirrooyfard 等人和 Chechik 等人的结果。

Conclusion: 本文通过重边技术成功突破了加权 n-Pairs 最短路径问题的近似比瓶颈，不仅回答了开放问题，还为后续研究提供了新的技术工具。

Abstract: Let $G = (V, E)$ be a graph with $n = |V|$ nodes and $m = |E|$ edges. The $t$-Pairs Shortest Paths problem, introduced by Cohen [FOCS'93; SICOMP'99], asks to approximate the distances between $t$ prespecified pairs of vertices. Recently, this problem has received renewed attention, particularly in the case where $t = Θ(n)$: the $n$-Pairs Shortest Paths problem. In this setting, new algorithms and conditional lower bounds have been developed by Dalirrooyfard, Jin, Vassilevska Williams, and Wein [FOCS'22], and Chechik, Hoch, and Lifshitz [SODA'25].
  In this paper, we present the first algorithm for the $n$-Pairs Shortest Paths problem in \textit{weighted} undirected graphs that achieves a $(2 - α)k$-approximation, for constant $α> 0$, that runs in $\tilde{O}(mn^{1/k} + n^{1 + 2/k})$ time. Specifically, we present a $1.622k$-approximation, improving upon the $(2k - 3)$-approximation of Chechik, Hoch, and Lifshitz [SODA'25] for graphs that are not super sparse, which answers in the affirmative the open question posed by them. We also develop improved approximation algorithms with better tradeoffs for unweighted graphs and dense weighted graphs that improve upon the results of Dalirrooyfard \etal~and Chechik, Hoch, and Lifshitz.
  Our main technical contribution is the new \textit{heavy-edge} technique. Using this technique, we transform an algorithm with an approximation guarantee that depends on $W_{uv}$, the weight of the heaviest edge on the shortest path between $u$ and $v$, into an algorithm with purely multiplicative approximation that does not depend on $W_{uv}$.

</details>

### [35] [Benchmarking Code Improvement with Progressive, Adaptive, and Interactive Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01360)
*Cuong Chi Le,Aashish Yadavally,Minh Le-Anh,Tien N. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出PAIR-Bench，一种通过渐进式提示结构来评估大语言模型代码改进能力（而非仅最终正确性）的基准测试框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于二元功能正确性的评估指标过于粗糙，忽略了代码修复过程中的部分进展、反馈利用、回归问题和改进轨迹等关键信息。

Method: 采用渐进式提示（progressive hinting）方法，包含两个控制维度：失败区域控制（确定反馈目标）和提示深度控制（决定透露多少修复信息），从而评估模型的修复能力、泛化能力、保持能力和所需辅助程度。

Result: 通过评估修复轨迹的渐进式指标（而非仅最终通过/失败结果），提供更细粒度的LLM代码改进能力评估。

Conclusion: PAIR-Bench能够更全面、更精细地衡量LLM在代码改进任务上的真实能力，超越传统的二元正确性评估范式。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically evaluated on code generation and program repair using binary functional correctness: a generated program or patch either passes or fails a test suite. This protocol is simple but coarse, as it ignores partial progress, feedback use, regressions, and the refinement trajectory through which models often improve code. We introduce PAIR-Bench, a progressive and adaptive benchmark for evaluating code improvement: transforming an incorrect or incomplete program into a more correct one through feedback-guided refinement. PAIR-Bench uses progressive hinting, a structured feedback protocol with two controls. Failure-region control determines what the feedback targets by grouping hidden failing tests into failure scenarios, while hint-depth control determines how much repair-relevant information is revealed, from coarse symptoms to implementation-level guidance. This design enables PAIR-Bench to measure whether a model repairs targeted failures, generalizes beyond the hint, preserves already-correct behavior, and how much assistance it requires. By evaluating repair trajectories progressive metrics rather than only final pass/fail outcomes, PAIR-Bench provides a finer-grained assessment of LLM code-improvement capability.

</details>


### [36] [A global predicted-fMRI drive signal from TRIBE does not predict YouTube replay heatmaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01400)
*Barada Sahu,Shivesh Pandey*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文评估了2025年Algonauts脑编码挑战赛冠军模型TRIBE（多模态深度学习模型）的预测结果与YouTube视频重播行为的关系。研究表明，该模型预测的皮层响应与视频“最重播”热力图之间几乎没有相关性（偏相关r=+0.058，p=0.23），且未显著优于简单的音量和运动基线。即使在六种皮层网络读数和自相关保留置换检验下，该结论依然成立。唯一的例外是音乐视频类型，存在片头/起始重播假象而非内容预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证深度多模态脑编码模型预测的神经信号是否能够预测真实世界中的行为（视频重播行为），从而检验这些模型是否真正捕捉到了与人类注意力或偏好相关的神经表征。

Method: 使用TRIBE模型（Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA2 + Wav2Vec-BERT）处理48个YouTube视频，将预测的皮层响应降维为每秒的全局场功率曲线，然后与YouTube平台收集的“最重播”热力图（被动收集的重播行为代理指标）进行相关性分析。使用位置控制偏相关、自相关保留置换检验等多种统计方法验证。

Result: 预测的皮层响应与重播行为之间无显著相关性：偏相关r=+0.058（95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]），不显著（p=0.23）。与简单基线（音量和运动）相比无显著提升。音乐视频中观察到的中等相关性是由于片头/起始重播假象，而非内容预测。结论在六种皮层网络读数和多重检验下保持稳健。

Conclusion: 当前最先进的多模态脑编码模型的预测神经信号不能预测视频重播行为，表明这些模型虽然能高精度预测fMRI响应，但尚未捕捉到与行为相关的神经表征。研究提醒相关领域需谨慎解读模型预测的行为含义。

Abstract: Deep multimodal brain-encoding models now predict fMRI responses to naturalistic video with high accuracy. Whether their predicted neural signals also forecast behavioral engagement is unknown. We run TRIBE, the winning model of the 2025 Algonauts brain-encoding challenge (Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA2 + Wav2Vec-BERT), on 48 YouTube videos and reduce its predicted cortical response to a per-second engagement curve, the global field power. Correlated against each video's "most replayed" heatmap, a passively-collected proxy for which moments viewers return to, the curve shows no evidence of predicting re-watch behavior. The pooled position-controlled partial correlation is +0.058 (95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]; one-sample t(47)=1.21, p=0.23), indistinguishable from zero and not significantly above simple loudness and motion baselines (loudness +0.04, paired p=0.74). The raw correlation is also near zero; the moderate values reported for music videos reflect a genre-specific intro/onset-replay artifact rather than content prediction, and do not generalize. The null holds across six cortical-network readouts and under an autocorrelation-preserving permutation test. We release the code, the video-ID manifest, and an acquisition method that works despite YouTube's SABR-only streaming.

</details>


### [37] [GPUAlert: A Zero-Instrumentation Process-Boundary Monitor for Diagnosing GPU Training-Job Failures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01409)
*Parv Agarwal,Asif Ekbal*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: GPUAlert是一个命令行包装器，能在不修改训练脚本的情况下监控GPU训练任务，通过进程边界的结构化通知提供失败原因分类、持久化日志和输出工件，并保证包装器的退出码与子进程状态一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GPU训练任务在大规模生产集群上失败率高达40%，但运维人员通常需要数小时后才能获知失败，现有解决方案（实验追踪器需修改脚本并保持云端连接；调度器邮件钩子仅提供单行状态而无原因和日志）无法有效解决这一问题。

Method: 提出三个可靠性原语：1）启动前日志保证（在子进程崩溃前建立持久化目标）；2）通知隔离（使包装器退出码是子进程状态的纯函数，与邮件发送是否成功无关）；3）非静默工件预算（限制附件大小但绝不静默丢弃输出）。还构建了包含15类失败、474个GPU训练日志的标注语料库和可复现评估工具。

Result: 在12个硬件可复现的失败类别上，有序规则分类器达到0.997 macro-F1（对比无序关键词匹配0.830和退出码检查0.133）；包装器开销恒定约3ms/任务；启动前日志保证在shell重定向无输出时仍能保存日志；在所有15种失败模式下，即使SMTP中继不可达，包装器仍保持子进程退出码不变。

Conclusion: GPUAlert通过轻量级、非侵入式的命令行包装方式，显著提升了GPU训练任务的失败检测与诊断能力，其三大可靠性原语确保了日志持久性、退出码正确性和输出完整性。

Abstract: GPU training jobs fail often, roughly two in five on large production clusters, yet the operator typically learns of a failure only by reconnecting hours later. Experiment trackers require editing the training script and maintaining a cloud connection; the scheduler's mail hook delivers a single status line with no cause and no logs. GPUAlert is a command-line wrapper that monitors any training command at the process boundary, and with no change to that command, emails a structured notification on completion carrying a classified failure cause, durable logs, and output artifacts. The tool is organized around three reliability primitives: a pre-launch log guarantee that establishes the durable destination before the child process can crash, notifier isolation that makes the wrapper's exit code a pure function of the child's status regardless of whether the email succeeds, and a non-silent artifact budget that bounds attachment size without ever dropping output silently. We release a labelled corpus of 474 GPU training logs across 15 failure classes and a reproducible evaluation harness. On the twelve hardware-reproduced classes, the ordered-rule classifier reaches 0.997 macro-F1, against 0.830 for unordered keyword matching and 0.133 for exit-code inspection. Wrapper overhead is a constant approximately 3ms per job; the pre-launch guarantee preserves a log where a shell redirect yields nothing; and across all 15 failure modes the wrapper returns the child's exit code unchanged even when the SMTP relay is unreachable.

</details>


### [38] [Adoption and Impact of Command-Line AI Coding Agents: A Study of Microsoft's Early 2026 Rollout of Claude Code and GitHub Copilot CLI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01418)
*Emerson Murphy-Hill,Jenna Butler,Alexandra Savelieva*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 微软早期2026年内部调研显示：AI命令行工具（如Claude Code/Copilot CLI）的首次使用主要通过社交网络传播，工程师的编码活跃度（而非人口统计特征）决定留存率，采用者合并PR数量比预期高出约24%，且该提升持续四个月。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业级部署AI命令行工具成本高昂（年token消耗可达数百万美元），管理者需要知道谁会试用、谁会持续使用、以及工具产出是否值得投入，以避免盲目推广带来的资源浪费。

Method: 对微软数万名工程师在2026年初的推广过程进行实证研究，分析社交网络传播模式、留存关联因素（编码活动 vs 人口统计）、以及采用者与未采用者的PR合并数量差异。

Result: 首次使用主要通过社交网络扩散；留存率与工程师的编码活跃度正相关，与人口统计特征无关；采用者合并的PR数量比基线多约24%，且该提升在四个月观测窗口内持续存在。

Conclusion: CLI编码智能体既非被均匀采用，也非短暂的新奇效应；组织应将可见的同行使用作为推广策略的核心。

Abstract: Organizations rolling out agentic command line tools like Anthropic's Claude Code and GitHub's Copilot CLI need to know who will try them, who will keep using them, and whether the tools produce enough output to justify their cost. At organizational scale, token spend can run into millions of dollars annually, so misreading adoption, retention, or impact can make a rollout expensive without changing engineering velocity. Studying tens of thousands of engineers at Microsoft over its early-2026 rollout, we find that first use spread primarily through social networks, retention was associated more with engineers' coding activity than with demographics, and adopters merged roughly 24% more pull requests than they would have otherwise. We use merged pull requests as our proxy for output -- acknowledging that a merged PR is not the same as the value it delivers -- and the lift persists across our four-month window. These results suggest that CLI coding agents are neither uniformly adopted nor mere novelty effects and that organizations should treat visible peer use as central to rollout strategy.

</details>


### [39] [Risk Architecture for AI-Native Engineering Teams: An Organizational Framework for Agentic System Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01421)
*Laxmipriya Ganesh Iyer*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文指出，传统软件工程风险管理框架（基于确定性、离散变更和明确归属）不适用于构建和运营Agentic AI系统的团队。论文提出了团队类型的七维画像、六类失效模式（含新发现的"依赖边界确定性失配"），以及合成框架充分性评估方法。研究发现，从纯软件工程到AI原生团队，风险覆盖单调下降，最严重且覆盖最差的失效出现在AI团队与被其视为确定的依赖方之间的组织边界上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件工程风险管理框架假定确定性行为、可审计的离散变更和清晰的组件所有者映射，但这些假设在Agentic AI系统中全部失效（输出概率性、自主多步行动、风险面静默突变）。政策层面（NIST AI RMF、ISO/IEC 42001）和威胁分类层面（OWASP）的文献并未从工程管理者的角色、决策权和升级结构视角提供指导，存在中层管理空白。

Method: 论文贡献了三项内容：(i) 七个维度的团队画像，区分纯软件工程团队、混合团队和AI原生团队；(ii) 六类失效模式分类法，其中包含此前未被阐述的"依赖边界确定性失配"类别；(iii) 一套合成框架充分性评估方法，对每种画像的风险架构在检测、遏制和升级预定义场景集方面的能力进行评分。由于研究对象是框架充分性而非人类行为，评估产生的是推导性而非观察性覆盖声明。

Result: 随着团队从纯软件工程向AI原生运作过渡，风险覆盖率中位数单调下降，且仅在AI原生团队阶段出现的高后果失效数量激增。退化集中在特定的失效模式类别。最严重且覆盖最差的失效并非出现在AI原生团队内部，而是出现在其概率性输出被假定确定性的依赖方消费的组织边界处。

Conclusion: 现有软件工程风险管理框架对AI原生团队严重不足，风险架构应特别关注AI团队与其依赖方之间的组织边界确定性失配问题，这是被现有文献忽略但后果最严重的关键缺口。

Abstract: Engineering management research has produced mature frameworks for software risk: ownership by feature, escalation by severity, and assurance by test coverage. These frameworks implicitly assume deterministic behavior, discrete and auditable change events, and clear component-to-owner mappings. Teams that build and operate agentic AI systems violate all three assumptions at once: outputs are probabilistic, systems take autonomous multi-step actions, and the risk surface mutates silently between deployments. Existing AI risk literature addresses this from above (policy frameworks such as the NIST AI RMF and ISO/IEC 42001) or below (threat taxonomies such as OWASP's agentic AI guidance), but not at the layer where an engineering manager (EM) operates: roles, decision rights, and escalation structures. This paper contributes (i) a seven-dimension profile distinguishing pure software-engineering, hybrid, and AI-native teams; (ii) a six-cluster failure-mode taxonomy including a previously unarticulated cluster, dependency-boundary determinism mismatch; and (iii) a synthetic framework-adequacy methodology scoring how well each profile's risk architecture detects, contains, and escalates a defined scenario set. Because the object of study is framework adequacy rather than human behavior, the evaluation yields derived rather than observed coverage claims. Coverage degrades as teams move from pure software engineering to AI-native operation, monotonically in the median and abruptly in the count of uncovered, high-consequence failures appearing only at the AI-native step. The degradation concentrates in specific failure-mode categories, and the most severe, least-covered failures arise not inside AI-native teams but at the organizational boundary where their probabilistic outputs are consumed by determinism-assuming dependencies.

</details>


### [40] [From Anatomy to Smells: An Empirical Study of SKILL.md in Agent Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01456)
*David Boram Hong,Aaron Imani,Iftekhar Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了LLM Agent Skills中的SKILL.md文件，通过对238个真实技能的分析，提炼出13个高层级和44个低层级的语义组件分类体系。同时通过文献综述识别最佳实践，提出"技能坏味"概念。自动检测发现超过99%的SKILL.md文件存在至少一个坏味，且一旦引入极少在演化中消失，揭示了实际编写与推荐实践之间的巨大差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent Skills被广泛使用，但SKILL.md文件如何编写、是否遵循现有指南，缺乏系统性研究。

Method: 1) 对238个真实世界SKILL.md文件进行定性分析，归纳出语义组件分类体系；2) 对29篇文献进行多来源文献综述，提取最佳实践并定义"技能坏味"；3) 开发自动化检测工具，对真实技能文件进行大规模检测。

Result: 提取了13个高层级、44个低层级语义组件；超99%的SKILL.md文件存在至少一个技能坏味，且坏味一旦引入极少在演化中消失。

Conclusion: 实际编写实践与推荐最佳实践之间存在显著差距，亟需开发自动化技术来修复技能坏味，并提高开发者对这一新兴质量问题的意识。

Abstract: Agent Skills provide on-demand domain knowledge to LLM agents without requiring model retraining. Each Agent Skill is defined by a mandatory SKILL.md file containing metadata and an unstructured Markdown body whose contents are left entirely to the skill author. Despite the rapid adoption of Agent Skills, little is known about how these files are authored or whether existing authoring guidelines are followed in practice. In this paper, we present the first systematic study of SKILL.md files as a software artifact. We qualitatively analyze 238 real-world skills and derive a taxonomy of 13 higher-level and 44 lower-level semantic components. We then conduct a multivocal literature review of 29 sources to identify best practices for authoring SKILL.md files and introduce skill smells as violations of these practices. Finally, we develop an automated detector and apply it to real-world skills, finding that over 99% of SKILL.md files contain at least one skill smell, and once introduced, skill smells rarely disappear as skills evolve. These findings reveal a substantial gap between recommended and actual authoring practices, motivating the development of automated techniques to remediate skill smells while increasing developer awareness of this emerging quality issue.

</details>


### [41] [Insights from GitHub Community on the Matter Standard: Developer Perspectives and Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01494)
*Muhammad Hassan,Carl Gunter,Susan Landau,Masooda Bashir*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过分析Project CHIP GitHub仓库中超过13,000个issue，研究开发者在使用Matter标准时遇到的四类主要问题：测试、互操作性、开发、平台与网络，并提出了改进测试基础设施、跨厂商指导与文档的具体建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: Matter标准仍面临系统性的技术挑战和集成难题，需要在测试基础设施、跨厂商指导和文档方面进行优化，以促进标准的成熟。

### [42] [Kani: A Model Checker for Rust](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01504)
*Rémi Delmas,Zyad Hassan,Qinheping Hu,Rahul Kumar,Felipe R. Monteiro,Thanh Nguyen,Adrián Palacios,Celina Val,Michael Tautschnig,Justus Adam,Daniel Schwartz-Narbonne,Carolyn Zech*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Kani是一个开源Rust模型检查器，通过将Rust MIR编译到CBMC引擎实现有界模型检查，支持函数契约、循环契约和函数存根等规范语言，可自动验证内存安全、功能正确性和无运行时恐慌等属性，已在工业项目中证明有效性，在Rust标准库验证中每次代码变更验证超过16,000个harness。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust的所有权类型系统虽然能防止安全代码中的内存错误，但许多关键属性（如unsafe操作的正确性、功能正确性和无运行时恐慌）仍然与编译正交，缺乏自动化的验证手段。

Method: 将Rust的MIR编译到CBMC的位精确验证引擎，自动检查安全属性；通过规范语言（函数契约、循环契约、量词、函数存根）将有界验证扩展到无界验证。

Result: 在工业Rust项目中，契约将验证从无恐慌性提升到功能正确性，发现6个先前未知的bug；在Rust标准库验证中每次代码变更运行超过16,000个验证harness。

Conclusion: Kani成功将Rust的验证从bug发现推进到正确性保证层面，能够在生产级CI中大规模运行，验证了模型检查在Rust生态中的实用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Rust's ownership type system prevents memory errors in safe code, but certain desirable properties remain orthogonal to compilation: the soundness of unsafe operations (e.g., raw pointer dereferences), functional correctness, and absence of runtime panics. We present Kani, an open-source model checker for Rust that pushes bounded model checking beyond bug-finding to provide correctness guarantees for these properties. Kani compiles proof harnesses from Rust's Mid-level Intermediate Representation (MIR) into CBMC's bit-precise verification engine, automatically checking a comprehensive set of safety properties with no user annotation. To extend verification from bounded to unbounded, Kani provides a specification language comprising function contracts, loop contracts, quantifiers, and function stubbing. We demonstrate feasibility through case studies on industrial Rust projects, where contracts upgraded verification from panic-freedom to functional correctness, uncovering six previously unknown bugs. Kani operates at scale in production CI, with over 16,000 harnesses verified per code change in the Rust standard library verification campaign.

Abstract: Classical software effort distribution models, including the PNR family and Parr alter native curve, were designed to describe the time distribution of development effort under an implied staffing pattern. This paper proposes a compact refactoring of Parr model as a capacity-aware forecasting layer for agile projects. The contribution is deliberately narrower than a full causal theory of project dynamics. A normalized Parr shaped latent effort demand is combined with an observed or planned capacity trajectory. The resulting model forecasts aggregate progress, completion time, capacity deficit, and capacity slack without assuming that the same internal activity path is followed under resource restriction. The model uses a small parameter set such as total effort K, a Parr shape parameter, an origin constant c that can match nonzero initial staffing, and the capacity trajectory. ### [44] [A Single Patch Is Not Enough: Deterministic Fusion of Repair Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01597)
*Boyang Yang,Xiangliang Hu,Luyao Ren,Yanjun Chen,Bach Le,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé,Haoye Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出PatchFusion，一种确定性原子证据融合方法，用于从候选补丁池中选择并构建最终补丁，无需测试或LLM评判，在SWE-bench等基准上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编码代理常用pass@k评估，但实际开发中只应用单个最终补丁，存在pass@k到pass@1的差距。现有后处理方法不能确定性地复用共享编辑原子证据来同时选择和构建最终补丁。

Method: PatchFusion采用确定性原子证据融合方法：首先将全差异一致性融合为修复邻域，选择可审计的代表性补丁，然后应用证据约束融合(ECF)保留重复编辑原子并剪枝不支持的部分。同时构建了包含SWE-bench Verified、SWE-bench Multilingual和Defects4J候选补丁的固定池基准PatchFuseBench。

Result: 在PatchFuseBench上，PatchFusion在SWE-bench Verified解决426/500个bug，SWE-bench Multilingual解决236/300个，Defects4J达到87/371个可信补丁，三项均优于所有候选池选择器。恢复41和27个单一源无法解决的bug。ECF增加+5/+6/+9个已解决bug且无回归。达到两个SWE-bench基准上候选可达上限的96.2%和89.7%。

Conclusion: 跨候选证据融合比基于测试和LLM的选择器能恢复更多正确补丁，且成本低几个数量级，证明确定性原子证据融合是有效的补丁后处理策略。

Abstract: Modern LLM coding agents are commonly evaluated using pass@k, but developers typically apply a single final patch in real-world settings. This pass@k-to-pass@1 gap is a post-generation problem: a candidate patch pool may contain a correct patch, but the system must decide which one to suggest to developers. Existing post-generation approaches mainly rank whole candidates, filter them with tests, or query an LLM judge, but none deterministically reuse shared edit-atom evidence to both select and construct the final patch. Thus, we propose PatchFusion, a deterministic atomic evidence fusion approach for candidate patches that consults no test outcome at decision time. PatchFusion first fuses whole-diff agreement into a repair neighborhood, selects an auditable representative, and then applies evidence-constrained fusion (ECF) to retain repeated edit atoms and prune unsupported parts. To evaluate this setting, we build PatchFuseBench, a fixed-pool benchmark covering SWE-bench Verified, SWE-bench Multilingual, and Defects4J candidate patches.
  On PatchFuseBench, PatchFusion solves 426/500 bugs on SWE-bench Verified and 236/300 on SWE-bench Multilingual, and reaches 87/371 plausible patches on Defects4J, outperforming every matched candidate-pool selector on all three. PatchFusion recovers 41 and 27 bugs that no single source solves (30 and 18 more over the best single source). Ablation studies show that ECF adds +5/+6/+9 solved bugs by recovering in-pool repairs that selection misses, with no observed regression, and that PatchFusion's gains remain stable as candidate pools are resampled. On these complementary multi-source pools, cross-candidate evidence recovers more correct patches than the test-based and LLM-based selectors we evaluate, at orders-of-magnitude lower cost, reaching within 96.2% and 89.7% of the candidate-reachable ceiling on the two SWE-bench benchmarks.

### [45] [AgentFlow: Building Agent Dependency Graphs for Static Analysis of Agent Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01640)
*Shenao Wang,Xinyi Hou,Yanjie Zhao,Xiao Cheng,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出AgentFlow，首个面向LLM代理程序的静态分析框架。它通过构建代理依赖图（ADG）来恢复代理程序中的框架语义依赖关系，支持代理物料清单生成和提示-工具风险检测，在5个框架和5,399个真实程序上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理程序依赖框架定义的语义（如模型、提示、工具、记忆和多代理编排逻辑），现有静态分析工具无法恢复这些新兴的代理依赖关系，导致难以对代理软件进行理解和安全治理。

Method: 提出AgentFlow框架，构建代理依赖图（ADG），将代理、提示、模型、能力、记忆状态和控制策略表示为类型化节点，将组件依赖、控制流和数据流依赖表示为类型化边。基于ADG支持代理物料清单（BOM）生成和提示-工具风险检测等分析。

Result: 在5个代表性代理框架和5,399个真实代理程序上评估，AgentFlow比现有AST工具恢复更丰富的代理实体和依赖关系，生成更完整的代理BOM，并发现238个真实世界代理程序中的污点式提示-工具风险。
